Benchmarks for decomposition¶

RandomizedPCA-arcene¶

Benchmark setup

from sklearn.decomposition import RandomizedPCA
from deps import load_data

kwargs = {'random_state': 0, 'n_components': 9}
X, y, X_t, y_t = load_data('arcene')
obj = RandomizedPCA(**kwargs)

Benchmark statement

obj.fit(X)

   337                                               def fit_transform(self, X, y=None, **fit_params):
   338                                                   """Fit to data, then transform it
   339
   340                                                   Fits transformer to X and y with optional parameters fit_params
   341                                                   and returns a transformed version of X.
   342
   343                                                   Parameters
   344                                                   ----------
   345                                                   X : numpy array of shape [n_samples, n_features]
   346                                                       Training set.
   347
   348                                                   y : numpy array of shape [n_samples]
   349                                                       Target values.
   350
   351                                                   Returns
   352                                                   -------
   353                                                   X_new : numpy array of shape [n_samples, n_features_new]
   354                                                       Transformed array.
   355
   356                                                   """
   357                                                   # non-optimized default implementation; override when a better
   358                                                   # method is possible for a given clustering algorithm
   359                                                   if y is None:
   360                                                       # fit method of arity 1 (unsupervised transformation)
   361                                                       return self.fit(X, **fit_params).transform(X)
   362                                                   else:
   363                                                       # fit method of arity 2 (supervised transformation)
   364                                                       return self.fit(X, y, **fit_params).transform(X)

   489                                                       self.components_ = V / S[:, np.newaxis] * np.sqrt(n)
   490                                                   else:
   491         2            5      2.5      0.0              self.components_ = V
   492
   493         2            3      1.5      0.0          return self

Line #      Hits         Time  Per Hit   % Time  Line Contents
==============================================================
   199                                               def fit_transform(self, X, y=None, **params):
   200                                                   """Fit the model with X and apply the dimensionality reduction on X.
   201
   202                                                   Parameters
   203                                                   ----------
   204                                                   X : array-like, shape (n_samples, n_features)
   205                                                       Training data, where n_samples in the number of samples
   206                                                       and n_features is the number of features.
   207
   208                                                   Returns
   209                                                   -------
   210                                                   X_new : array-like, shape (n_samples, n_components)
   211
   212                                                   """
   213                                                   U, S, V = self._fit(X, **params)
   214                                                   U = U[:, :self.n_components]
   215
   216                                                   if self.whiten:
   217                                                       # X_new = X * V / S * sqrt(n_samples) = U * sqrt(n_samples)
   218                                                       U *= np.sqrt(X.shape[0])
   219                                                   else:
   220                                                       # X_new = X * V = U * S * V^T * V = U * S
   221                                                       U *= S[:self.n_components]
   222
   223                                                   return U

==============================================================
   199                                               def fit_transform(self, X, y=None, **params):
   200                                                   """Fit the model with X and apply the dimensionality reduction on X.
   201
   202                                                   Parameters
   203                                                   ----------
   204                                                   X : array-like, shape (n_samples, n_features)
   205                                                       Training data, where n_samples in the number of samples
   206                                                       and n_features is the number of features.
   207
   208                                                   Returns
   209                                                   -------
   210                                                   X_new : array-like, shape (n_samples, n_components)
   211
   212                                                   """
   213                                                   U, S, V = self._fit(X, **params)
   214                                                   U = U[:, :self.n_components]
   215
   216                                                   if self.whiten:
   217                                                       # X_new = X * V / S * sqrt(n_samples) = U * sqrt(n_samples)
   218                                                       U *= np.sqrt(X.shape[0])
   219                                                   else:
   220                                                       # X_new = X * V = U * S * V^T * V = U * S
   221                                                       U *= S[:self.n_components]
   222
   223                                                   return U

   193                                               def fit_transform(self, X, y=None, **params):
   194                                                   """Fit the model from data in X and transform X.
   195
   196                                                   Parameters
   197                                                   ----------
   198                                                   X: array-like, shape (n_samples, n_features)
   199                                                       Training vector, where n_samples in the number of samples
   200                                                       and n_features is the number of features.
   201
   202                                                   Returns
   203                                                   -------
   204                                                   X_new: array-like, shape (n_samples, n_components)
   205                                                   """
   206                                                   self.fit(X, **params)
   207
   208                                                   X_transformed = self.alphas_ * np.sqrt(self.lambdas_)
   209
   210                                                   if self.fit_inverse_transform:
   211                                                       self._fit_inverse_transform(X_transformed, X)

   213                                                   return X_transformed

Line #      Hits         Time  Per Hit   % Time  Line Contents
==============================================================
   458                                               def fit_transform(self, X, y=None):
   459                                                   """Learn a NMF model for the data X and returns the transformed data.
   460
   461                                                   This is more efficient than calling fit followed by transform.
   462
   463                                                   Parameters
   464                                                   ----------
   465
   466                                                   X: {array-like, sparse matrix}, shape = [n_samples, n_features]
   467                                                       Data matrix to be decomposed
   468
   469                                                   Returns
   470                                                   -------
   471                                                   data: array, [n_samples, n_components]
   472                                                       Transformed data
   473                                                   """
   474         1          280    280.0      0.0          X = atleast2d_or_csr(X)
   475         1          128    128.0      0.0          check_non_negative(X, "NMF.fit")
   476
   477         1            5      5.0      0.0          n_samples, n_features = X.shape
   478
   479         1            4      4.0      0.0          if not self.n_components:
   480                                                       self.n_components = n_features
   481
   482         1        16162  16162.0      0.6          W, H = self._init(X)
   483
   484         1          129    129.0      0.0          gradW = (np.dot(W, np.dot(H, H.T))
   485         1          335    335.0      0.0                   - safe_sparse_dot(X, H.T, dense_output=True))
   486         1          139    139.0      0.0          gradH = (np.dot(np.dot(W.T, W), H)
   487         1          243    243.0      0.0                   - safe_sparse_dot(W.T, X, dense_output=True))
   488         1          289    289.0      0.0          init_grad = norm(np.r_[gradW, gradH.T])
   489         1           14     14.0      0.0          tolW = max(0.001, self.tol) * init_grad  # why max?
   490         1            3      3.0      0.0          tolH = tolW
   491
   492       201          706      3.5      0.0          for n_iter in xrange(1, self.max_iter + 1):
   493                                                       # stopping condition
   494                                                       # as discussed in paper
   495       200        51389    256.9      2.0              proj_norm = norm(np.r_[gradW[np.logical_or(gradW < 0, W > 0)],
   496       200        87868    439.3      3.4                                     gradH[np.logical_or(gradH < 0, H > 0)]])
   497       200         2416     12.1      0.1              if proj_norm < self.tol * init_grad:
   498                                                           break
   499
   500                                                       # update W

   549                                               def transform(self, X):
   550                                                   """Transform the data X according to the fitted NMF model
   551
   552                                                   Parameters
   553                                                   ----------
   554
   555                                                   X: {array-like, sparse matrix}, shape = [n_samples, n_features]
   556                                                       Data matrix to be transformed by the model
   557
   558                                                   Returns
   559                                                   -------
   560                                                   data: array, [n_samples, n_components]
   561                                                       Transformed data
   562                                                   """
   563                                                   X = atleast2d_or_csr(X)
   564                                                   H = np.zeros((X.shape[0], self.n_components))
   565                                                   for j in xrange(0, X.shape[0]):
   566                                                       H[j, :], _ = nnls(self.components_.T, X[j, :])
   567                                                   return H

   337                                               def fit_transform(self, X, y=None, **fit_params):
   338                                                   """Fit to data, then transform it
   339
   340                                                   Fits transformer to X and y with optional parameters fit_params
   341                                                   and returns a transformed version of X.
   342
   343                                                   Parameters
   344                                                   ----------
   345                                                   X : numpy array of shape [n_samples, n_features]
   346                                                       Training set.
   347
   348                                                   y : numpy array of shape [n_samples]
   349                                                       Target values.
   350
   351                                                   Returns
   352                                                   -------
   353                                                   X_new : numpy array of shape [n_samples, n_features_new]
   354                                                       Transformed array.
   355
   356                                                   """
   357                                                   # non-optimized default implementation; override when a better
   358                                                   # method is possible for a given clustering algorithm
   359                                                   if y is None:
   360                                                       # fit method of arity 1 (unsupervised transformation)
   361                                                       return self.fit(X, **fit_params).transform(X)
   362                                                   else:
   363                                                       # fit method of arity 2 (supervised transformation)
   364                                                       return self.fit(X, y, **fit_params).transform(X)

   698                                               def transform(self, X, y=None):
   699                                                   """Encode the data as a sparse combination of the dictionary atoms.
   700
   701                                                   Coding method is determined by the object parameter
   702                                                   `transform_algorithm`.
   703
   704                                                   Parameters
   705                                                   ----------
   706                                                   X : array of shape (n_samples, n_features)
   707                                                       Test data to be transformed, must have the same number of
   708                                                       features as the data used to train the model.
   709
   710                                                   Returns
   711                                                   -------
   712                                                   X_new : array, shape (n_samples, n_components)
   713                                                       Transformed data
   714
   715                                                   """
   716                                                   # XXX : kwargs is not documented
   717                                                   X = array2d(X)
   718                                                   n_samples, n_features = X.shape
   719
   720                                                   code = sparse_encode(
   721                                                       X, self.components_, algorithm=self.transform_algorithm,
   722                                                       n_nonzero_coefs=self.transform_n_nonzero_coefs,
   723                                                       alpha=self.transform_alpha, n_jobs=self.n_jobs)
   724
   725                                                   if self.split_sign:
   726                                                       # feature vector is split into a positive and negative side
   727                                                       n_samples, n_features = code.shape
   728                                                       split_code = np.empty((n_samples, 2 * n_features))
   729                                                       split_code[:, :n_features] = np.maximum(code, 0)
   730                                                       split_code[:, n_features:] = -np.minimum(code, 0)
   731                                                       code = split_code
   732
   733                                                   return code

   337                                               def fit_transform(self, X, y=None, **fit_params):
   338                                                   """Fit to data, then transform it
   339
   340                                                   Fits transformer to X and y with optional parameters fit_params
   341                                                   and returns a transformed version of X.
   342
   343                                                   Parameters
   344                                                   ----------
   345                                                   X : numpy array of shape [n_samples, n_features]
   346                                                       Training set.
   347
   348                                                   y : numpy array of shape [n_samples]
   349                                                       Target values.
   350
   351                                                   Returns
   352                                                   -------
   353                                                   X_new : numpy array of shape [n_samples, n_features_new]
   354                                                       Transformed array.
   355
   356                                                   """
   357                                                   # non-optimized default implementation; override when a better
   358                                                   # method is possible for a given clustering algorithm
   359                                                   if y is None:
   360                                                       # fit method of arity 1 (unsupervised transformation)
   361                                                       return self.fit(X, **fit_params).transform(X)
   362                                                   else:
   363                                                       # fit method of arity 2 (supervised transformation)
   364                                                       return self.fit(X, y, **fit_params).transform(X)

   337                                               def fit_transform(self, X, y=None, **fit_params):
   338                                                   """Fit to data, then transform it
   339
   340                                                   Fits transformer to X and y with optional parameters fit_params
   341                                                   and returns a transformed version of X.
   342
   343                                                   Parameters
   344                                                   ----------
   345                                                   X : numpy array of shape [n_samples, n_features]
   346                                                       Training set.
   347
   348                                                   y : numpy array of shape [n_samples]
   349                                                       Target values.
   350
   351                                                   Returns
   352                                                   -------
   353                                                   X_new : numpy array of shape [n_samples, n_features_new]
   354                                                       Transformed array.
   355
   356                                                   """
   357                                                   # non-optimized default implementation; override when a better
   358                                                   # method is possible for a given clustering algorithm
   359                                                   if y is None:
   360                                                       # fit method of arity 1 (unsupervised transformation)
   361                                                       return self.fit(X, **fit_params).transform(X)
   362                                                   else:
   363                                                       # fit method of arity 2 (supervised transformation)
   364                                                       return self.fit(X, y, **fit_params).transform(X)
